Bank or Institution City sucursal Swift Code COUNTRY_ID
	
CREATE TABLE `swift` (
  `SWIFT_PK` int(11) NOT NULL auto_increment,
  `SW_BANK` varchar(200) NOT NULL,
  `SW_CITY` varchar(200) default NULL,
  `SW_BRANCH` varchar(200) default NULL,
  `SW_CODE` char(11) NOT NULL,
  `SW_COUNTRY_ID` int(6) NOT NULL
  PRIMARY KEY  (`SWIFT_PK`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1 AUTO_INCREMENT=3838 ;
